  <script>
    window.filterCharm = (params) => {
      let output = window.dataSource;
      if (!params.skill1 && !params.skill2 && !params.skill3) {
        alert("请输入至少一个技能名称");
        return;
      }
      if (params.rare) {
        output = output.filter((item) => item._Rare === params.rare);
      }
      if (params.skill1) {
        output = output.filter((item) => {
          return item._SkillPt_01_SkillList.includes(
            `${params.skill1}Lv${params.skill1Lv}`
          );
        });
      }
      if (params.skill2) {
        output = output.filter((item) => {
          return item._SkillPt_02_SkillList.includes(
            `${params.skill2}Lv${params.skill2Lv}`
          );
        });
      }
      if (params.skill3) {
        output = output.filter((item) => {
          return item._SkillPt_03_SkillList.includes(
            `${params.skill3}Lv${params.skill3Lv}`
          );
        });
      }
      if (params.slot) {
        output = output.filter(
          (item) => item._SlotPt_SlotDescription === params.slot
        );
      }
      return output.map((item) => {
        return {
          id: item._Index,
          rare: item._Rare,
          skill1: item._SkillPt_01_SkillList.join(", "),
          skill2: item._SkillPt_02_SkillList.join(", "),
          skill3: item._SkillPt_03_SkillList.join(", "),
          slot: item._SlotPt_SlotDescription,
        };
      });
    };
  </script>
  <script>
    function renderListToTable(dataList) {
      const resultContainer = document.getElementById("result");

      // 创建表格元素
      const table = document.createElement("table");
      table.border = "1"; // 添加边框（可选）

      // 1. 创建表头（<thead>）
      const thead = document.createElement("thead");
      const headerRow = document.createElement("tr");

      // 假设列表第一项包含表头字段名（动态提取）
      const headers = Object.keys(dataList[0] || {});
      headers.forEach((headerText) => {
        const th = document.createElement("th");
        th.textContent = headerText;
        headerRow.appendChild(th);
      });
      thead.appendChild(headerRow);
      table.appendChild(thead);

      // 2. 创建表格内容（<tbody>）
      const tbody = document.createElement("tbody");
      dataList.forEach((item) => {
        const row = document.createElement("tr");
        headers.forEach((header) => {
          const td = document.createElement("td");
          td.textContent = item[header]; // 填充单元格数据
          row.appendChild(td);
        });
        tbody.appendChild(row);
      });
      table.appendChild(tbody);

      // 将表格添加到页面
      resultContainer.innerHTML = ""; // 清空容器
      resultContainer.appendChild(table);
    }
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
      const form = document.getElementById("query-form");
      form.addEventListener("submit", function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const formData = new FormData(form);
        const formValues = Object.fromEntries(formData.entries());
        const queryOutput = window.filterCharm(formValues);
        if (queryOutput.length === 0) {
          alert("没有符合条件的护石");
          return;
        }
        renderListToTable(
          queryOutput.map((item) => ({
            模板ID: item.id,
            稀有度: item.rare,
            护石1技能列表: item.skill1,
            护石2技能列表: item.skill2,
            护石3技能列表: item.skill3,
            护石装饰孔: item.slot,
          }))
        );
      });
    });
  </script>
</body>
